copy_pretender_empire_effect = { # Character scope
	e_china = {
		save_dynasty_name_effect = yes
		
		clear_all_chinese_dynasty_flags_and_update_global_flags_effect = yes
		
		ROOT = {
			primary_title = {
				e_china = {
					copy_title_laws = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		
		make_primary_title = yes
	}
	
	any_demesne_title = {
		limit = {
			tier = emperor
			has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
			is_primary_holder_title = no
		}
		
		copy_pretender_empire_name_effect = yes
		
		unsafe_destroy_landed_title = THIS
		
		add_pressed_claim = PREV
	}
	
	e_china = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					has_character_flag = chinese_succession
				}
			}
			
			add_law = {
				law = succ_chinese_imperial_succession
				cooldown = no
				opinion_effect = no
			}
			
			ROOT = {
				clr_character_flag = chinese_succession
			}
		}
		
		else = {
			add_law = {
				law = succ_primogeniture
				cooldown = no
				opinion_effect = no
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Conclave"
			}
			
			add_law = {
				law = ze_administration_laws_2
				cooldown = no
				opinion_effect = no
			}
		}
		
		else = {
			add_law = {
				law = imperial_administration
				cooldown = no
				opinion_effect = no
			}
		}
		
		# All non-GC laws shift two steps towards depowering, GC one step
		trigger_switch = {
			on_trigger = has_law
			
			eunuch_law_4 = { add_law = eunuch_law_2 }
			eunuch_law_3 = { add_law = eunuch_law_1 }
			eunuch_law_2 = { add_law = eunuch_law_0 }
			eunuch_law_1 = { add_law = eunuch_law_0 }
		}
		
		trigger_switch = {
			on_trigger = has_law
			
			grand_chancellor_law_2 = { add_law = grand_chancellor_law_1 }
			grand_chancellor_law_1 = { add_law = grand_chancellor_law_0 }
		}
		
		trigger_switch = {
			on_trigger = has_law
			
			ci_courtier_law_4 = { add_law = ci_courtier_law_2 }
			ci_courtier_law_3 = { add_law = ci_courtier_law_1 }
			ci_courtier_law_2 = { add_law = ci_courtier_law_0 }
			ci_courtier_law_1 = { add_law = ci_courtier_law_0 }
		}
		
		trigger_switch = {
			on_trigger = has_law
			
			ci_vassal_law_4 = { add_law = ci_vassal_law_2 }
			ci_vassal_law_3 = { add_law = ci_vassal_law_1 }
			ci_vassal_law_2 = { add_law = ci_vassal_law_0 }
			ci_vassal_law_1 = { add_law = ci_vassal_law_0 }
		}
	}
}

create_real_chinese_imperial_bloodline_title_scope_effect = { # Title scope
	holder_scope = {
		create_real_chinese_imperial_bloodline_effect = yes
	}
}

create_real_chinese_imperial_bloodline_effect = { # Character scope
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOR = {
				any_owned_bloodline = {
					has_bloodline_flag = real_chinese_imperial_bloodline
					founder = {
						character = PREVPREV
					}
				}
				has_character_flag = was_chinese_imperial
			}
		}
		
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = create_real_ci_bloodline
			
			set_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty # Important for temple names!
			
			primary_title = {
				trigger_switch = {
					on_trigger = has_title_flag
					
					ba_china = {
						ROOT = {
							if = {
								limit = {
									is_female = no
								}
								create_bloodline = {
									type = real_chinese_imperial_bloodline_ba
								}
							}
							else = {
								create_bloodline = {
									type = real_chinese_imperial_bloodline_ba
									inheritance = matrilineal
								}
							}
						}
						
						set_global_flag = china_has_been_ba_china
					}
					
					bei_china = {
						ROOT = {
							if = {

china_usurpation_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			e_china = {
				capital_scope = {
					holder_scope = {
						OR = {
							character = ROOT
							any_liege = {
								character = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
			# Don't game over the player
			ROOT = {
				OR = {
					ai = yes
					any_demesne_title = {
						tier = count
						count = 2
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		e_china = {
			capital_scope = {
				county = {
					save_event_target_as = capital_of_china
				}
			}
		}
		
		event_target:capital_of_china = {
			usurp_title = FROM
			add_pressed_claim = ROOT
		}
	}
	
	any_vassal = {
		limit = {
			higher_real_tier_than = baron
		}
		set_defacto_liege = e_china
	}
	
	any_demesne_title = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				tier = king
				tier = duke
			}
			controls_religion = no
		}
		unsafe_destroy_landed_title = THIS
		add_pressed_claim = PREV
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			e_china = {
				holder_scope = {
					OR = {
						dynasty = ROOT
						is_close_relative = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		any_tributary = {
			decrease_tributary_tier_or_release_effect = yes
		}
	}
	
	else = {
		any_tributary = {
			ROOT = {
				remove_tributary = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	
	disband_event_forces = longwu_guard
	disband_event_forces = longwei_guard
	disband_event_forces = pengri_guard
	disband_event_forces = shence_guard
	disband_event_forces = shenwei_guard
	disband_event_forces = shenwu_guard
	disband_event_forces = tianwu_guard
	disband_event_forces = yulin_guard
	
	remove_character_modifier = longwu_guard_raised
	remove_character_modifier = longwei_guard_raised
	remove_character_modifier = pengri_guard_raised
	remove_character_modifier = shence_guard_raised
	remove_character_modifier = shenwei_guard_raised
	remove_character_modifier = shenwu_guard_raised
	remove_character_modifier = tianwu_guard_raised
	remove_character_modifier = yulin_guard_raised
}

clean_up_all_chinese_pretenders_effect = { # Character scope
	any_title = {
		limit = {
			tier = emperor
			has_holder = no
			OR = {
				title = e_china
				has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
			}
		}
		
		clear_all_chinese_dynasty_flags_and_update_global_flags_effect = yes
	}
}

clean_up_chinese_pretender_effect = { # Character scope
	primary_title = {
		clear_all_chinese_dynasty_flags_and_update_global_flags_effect = yes
	}
}

clean_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = { # Any scope
	custom_tooltip = {
		text = clean_up_grace
		
		any_character = { # Necessary, if expensive
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_character_flag = grace_character
					trait = dragon_bride_unmarried
					trait = dragon_bride_married
					has_character_modifier = peace_deal_with_china
					has_character_flag = not_a_dragon_bride
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_1
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_2
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_3
					trait = kow_tow_travels
				}
			}
			
			set_variable = {
				which = grace
				value = 0
			}
			
			clr_character_flag = grace_character
			clr_character_flag = not_a_dragon_bride
			remove_trait = dragon_bride_unmarried
			remove_trait = dragon_bride_married
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_1
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_2
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_3
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = preparing_treasure_fleet
					has_global_flag = treasure_fleet_is_active
					has_global_flag = treasure_fleet_invasion_ongoing
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = treasure_fleet_abort_china
			2753 = {
				set_province_flag = abort_treasure_fleet_asap
			}
		}
	}
	
	clr_global_flag = longwei_guard_eunuchs
	clr_global_flag = longwei_guard_exists
	clr_global_flag = longwu_guard_eunuchs
	clr_global_flag = longwu_guard_exists
	clr_global_flag = pengri_guard_eunuchs
	clr_global_flag = pengri_guard_exists
	clr_global_flag = shence_guard_eunuchs
	clr_global_flag = shence_guard_exists
	clr_global_flag = shenwei_guard_eunuchs
	clr_global_flag = shenwei_guard_exists
	clr_global_flag = shenwu_guard_eunuchs
	clr_global_flag = shenwu_guard_exists
	clr_global_flag = tianwu_guard_eunuchs
	clr_global_flag = tianwu_guard_exists
	clr_global_flag = yulin_guard_eunuchs
	clr_global_flag = yulin_guard_exists
	
	any_playable_ruler = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_earmarked_regiments = longwu_guard
				has_earmarked_regiments = longwei_guard
				has_earmarked_regiments = pengri_guard
				has_earmarked_regiments = shence_guard
				has_earmarked_regiments = shenwei_guard
				has_earmarked_regiments = shenwu_guard
				has_earmarked_regiments = tianwu_guard
				has_earmarked_regiments = yulin_guard
				has_character_modifier = longwu_guard_raised
				has_character_modifier = longwei_guard_raised
				has_character_modifier = pengri_guard_raised
				has_character_modifier = shence_guard_raised
				has_character_modifier = shenwei_guard_raised
				has_character_modifier = shenwu_guard_raised
				has_character_modifier = tianwu_guard_raised
				has_character_modifier = yulin_guard_raised
			}
		}
		
		disband_event_forces = longwu_guard
		disband_event_forces = longwei_guard
		disband_event_forces = pengri_guard
		disband_event_forces = shence_guard
		disband_event_forces = shenwei_guard
		disband_event_forces = shenwu_guard
		disband_event_forces = tianwu_guard
		disband_event_forces = yulin_guard
		
	
		remove_character_modifier = longwu_guard_raised
		remove_character_modifier = longwei_guard_raised
		remove_character_modifier = pengri_guard_raised
		remove_character_modifier = shence_guard_raised
		remove_character_modifier = shenwei_guard_raised
		remove_character_modifier = shenwu_guard_raised
		remove_character_modifier = tianwu_guard_raised
		remove_character_modifier = yulin_guard_raised
	}
	
	any_independent_ruler = {
		limit = {
			any_war = {
				OR = {
					using_cb = treasure_fleet_punitive_expedition
					using_cb = treasure_fleet_tributary_war
				}
			}
		}
		
		any_war = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					using_cb = treasure_fleet_punitive_expedition
					using_cb = treasure_fleet_tributary_war
				}
			}
			
			end_war = invalid
		}
	}
}

set_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = { # Character scope
	custom_tooltip = {
		text = set_up_grace
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_law = agnatic_succession
				}
				
				has_dlc = "Jade Dragon"
				
				has_game_rule = {
					name = imperial_marriages
					value = enabled
				}
			}
			
			any_dynasty_member = {
				limit = {
					is_female = yes
					is_landed = no
					
					employer = {
						OR = {
							character = ROOT
							
							top_liege = {
								character = ROOT
							}
							
							liege_before_war = {
								character = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_married = yes
							is_consort = yes
						}
					}
					remove_trait = dragon_bride_unmarried
					
					add_trait = dragon_bride_married
				}
				
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_character_flag = not_a_dragon_bride
						}
					}
					
					add_trait = dragon_bride_unmarried
				}
			}
		}
		
		else = {
			any_dynasty_member = {
				limit = {
					is_female = yes
				}
				
				remove_trait = dragon_bride_married
				
				remove_trait = dragon_bride_unmarried
			}
		}
	}
}

copy_old_dynasty_flag_from_old_eoc_effect = { # Character scope
	event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
		copy_old_dynasty_flag_from_me_effect = yes
	}
}
